<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;"><b>Item 2.02 Results of Operations and Financial Condition</b></div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#xa0;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">On&#xa0;November 14, 2023,&#xa0; ParkerVision, Inc. (the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release which reported financial and operating results for the three and nine months ended September 30, 2023. A copy of the press release is attached as Exhibit 99.1 and is incorporated herein by reference.</div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#xa0;</div>

<div style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -1pt;">The information contained in this Current Report on Form 8-K, including Exhibit 99.1 hereto, has been &#8220;furnished&#8221; and shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for purposes of Section 18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended, or otherwise subject to liability under that section. The information in this Current Report shall not be incorporated by reference into any filing or other document pursuant to the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, except as shall be expressly set forth by specific reference in such filing or document.</div>

<div style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 10pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt -9pt;">&#xa0;</div>

<body style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 10pt; padding: 0in 0.1in; cursor: auto;">
<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: right; font-size: 11pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;"><font style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif; font-size: 11pt;"><b>&nbsp;Exhibit 99.1</b></font></p>

<p style="margin: 0pt; text-align: left; font-size: 10pt; font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;, Times, serif;"><font style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 10pt">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 14pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: center; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b>ParkerVision Reports $10.6 Million in Net Income for First Nine Months of 2023 </b></p>

<p style="font-family:'Times New Roman';font-size:10pt;font-variant:normal;margin:0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b>JACKSONVILLE</b><b>, Fla.,&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="21x1" data-tblname="384392" data-tblv="2" id="led384392F20232231679594614065">November 14, 2023</a> </b>&#8211;<b> </b>ParkerVision, Inc. (OTCQB: PRKR) (&#8220;ParkerVision&#8221; or the "Company"), a developer and marketer of technologies and products for wireless applications, today announced results for the three and <a data-tblloc="13x1" data-tblname="384392" data-tblv="2" id="led384392F20232231679594637533">nine months ended September 30, 2023</a>.</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b><i>&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="384391" data-tblv="2" id="led384391F20232231679594669899">2023</a>&nbsp;Summary and Recent Developments</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">On November 6, 2023, oral arguments were heard by the United States Court of Appeals for the Federal Circuit (CAFC) in <i>ParkerVision v. Qualcomm.&nbsp; </i>The parties are awaiting the CAFC's decisions.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 72.6px;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 25px;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: 1656px; font-size: 11pt;">The Company appealed three separate rulings made in March 2022 by the district court in the Middle District of Florida (Orlando division) in the Company's patent infringement case against Qualcomm.</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px; font-size: 11pt;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top; font-size: 11pt;">
			<td style="width: 36pt; font-size: 11pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt; font-size: 11pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto; font-size: 11pt;">The Company recognized $25 million in revenue from patent license and settlement agreements in 2023 and, after recognizing contingent legal fees and expenses, reported net income of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x5" data-tblname="456620" data-tblv="9" id="led456620F20231091699546534255">$10.6</a> million for the nine months ended September 30, 2023.</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The Company successfully negotiated the extension of maturity dates on $1.2 million of convertible notes that were scheduled to mature from September 2023 through March 2024.&nbsp;&nbsp; These notes now mature in February/March 2026.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">Jeffrey Parker, Chairman and Chief Executive Officer, commented, &#8220;ParkerVision was eager to present its arguments to the CAFC last week, and we believe key points supporting reversal that were contained in our appellate briefs to the CAFC were discussed in the hearing.&nbsp;&nbsp; We are hopeful that the CAFC will reverse the district court's prior rulings and remand our case back to Florida district court. &nbsp; Meanwhile, the four active patent infringement cases in the Western District of Texas against Realtek, MediaTek, NXP, and Texas Instruments continue to progress.&nbsp; Claim construction hearings are scheduled in January 2024 in the Realtek and MediaTek cases."</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;">&#65279;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt 0pt 0pt 8pt;"><b><i>Financial Results</i></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">ParkerVision reported a net loss for the third quarter of <a data-tblloc="0x1" data-tblname="384391" data-tblv="2" id="led384391F20232231679594889334">2023</a> of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x1" data-tblname="456620" data-tblv="9" id="led456620F20231081699480488496">$3.9</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x1" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="2" id="led384395F2023731691091818046">$0.05</a> per common share, compared to a net loss of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x2" data-tblname="456620" data-tblv="9" id="led456620F20231081699480505072">$0.4</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x2" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="2" id="led384395F2023731691091908522">$0.01</a> per common share for the third quarter of <a data-tblloc="32x1" data-tblname="384391" data-tblv="2" id="led384391F20232231679594923115">2022</a>.&nbsp; The increase in net loss is largely the result of an increase in the estimated fair value of contingent payment obligations.&nbsp;</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">ParkerVision reported net income of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x5" data-tblname="456620" data-tblv="9" id="led456620F20231081699480601739">$10.6</a> million for the first nine months of 2023, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x5" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="2" id="led384395F2023731691092876837">$0.12</a> per common share, compared to a net loss of&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="3x6" data-tblname="456620" data-tblv="9" id="led456620F20231081699480620277">$4.5</a> million, or&nbsp;<a data-tblloc="2x6" data-tblname="384395" data-tblv="2" id="led384395F2023731691092959844">$0.06</a> per common share for the first nine months of 2022.&nbsp; The increase in net income is primarily the result of $25 million in revenue recognized on a patent license and settlement agreement reached in February 2023, offset by contingent legal fees and expenses incurred related to the agreement.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

		<tr style="vertical-align: top;">
			<td style="width: 36pt;">&nbsp;</td>
			<td style="width: 18pt;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&#9679;</p>
			</td>
			<td style="width: auto;">
			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">During the first nine months of 2023, the Company repaid $13.9 million of its secured contingent payment obligation with proceeds received from patent license and settlement agreements and received $5.0 million in new contingent borrowings.</p>
			</td>
		</tr>

</table>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<table border="0" cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="width: 100%; text-indent: 0px;">

			<p style="font-family: 'Times New Roman', Times, serif; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">The Company had $3.3 million in cash and cash equivalents as of September 30, 2023.&nbsp;</p>
			</td>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;"><b><u>About ParkerVision</u></b></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>

<p style="font-family: Times New Roman; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; text-align: justify; margin: 0pt;">ParkerVision, Inc. invents, develops and licenses cutting-edge, proprietary radio-frequency (RF) technologies that enable wireless solution providers to make and sell advanced wireless communication products. &nbsp;ParkerVision is engaged in a number of patent enforcement actions in the U.S. to protect patented rights that it believes are broadly infringed by others. For more information, please visit www.parkervision.com.<i> (PRKR-I)</i></p>

<p style="font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;; font-size: 11pt; font-variant: normal; margin: 0pt;">&nbsp;</p>
